@compiletime function create_w3b_Icon()
	let u = createObjectDefinition("w3b", 'Icon', 'YTlb')
	u.setReal("bgsc", 0.0)
	u.setString("bshd", "")
	u.setInt("bcpd", 0)
	u.setString("bsuf", "Blood Mage")
	u.setUnreal("boch", 0.0)
	u.setUnreal("bsel", 0.0)
	u.setString("bfil", "none.mdl")
	u.setString("bnam", "(Icon)")
	u.setString("barm", "Ethereal")
	u.setString("btar", "")
	u.setInt("bcpr", 0)
	u.setString("bptx", "")
	u.setInt("btxi", 31)
	u.setUnreal("bmas", 10.0)
	u.setUnreal("bmis", 10.0)
	u.setInt("bvcr", 135)

	u.setInt("wurs", 42)
	u.setReal("bgsc", 0.0)
	u.setString("bshd", "")
	u.setInt("bcpd", 0)
	u.setString("bsuf", "Icon")
	u.setUnreal("boch", 0.0)
	u.setUnreal("bsel", 0.0)
	u.setString("bfil", "war3mapImported\\ButtonC.mdl")
	u.setString("bnam", "EarthBrewMaster")
	u.setString("barm", "Ethereal")
	u.setString("btar", "")
	u.setInt("bcpr", 0)
	u.setString("bptx", "")
	u.setInt("btxi", 31)
	u.setString("btxf", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNEarthBrewMaster.blp")
	u.setInt("bvcr", 76)
	u.setInt("bvcg", 76)
	u.setInt("bvcb", 76)

	u.setInt("wurs", 42)
	u.setReal("bgsc", 0.0)
	u.setString("bshd", "")
	u.setInt("bcpd", 0)
	u.setString("bsuf", "Icon")
	u.setUnreal("boch", 0.0)
	u.setUnreal("bsel", 0.0)
	u.setString("bfil", "war3mapImported\\ButtonC.mdl")
	u.setString("bnam", "MarkOfFire")
	u.setString("barm", "Ethereal")
	u.setString("btar", "")
	u.setInt("bcpr", 0)
	u.setString("bptx", "")
	u.setInt("btxi", 31)
	u.setString("btxf", "ReplaceableTextures\\CommandButtons\\BTNMarkOfFire.blp")
	u.setInt("bvcr", 76)
	u.setInt("bvcg", 76)
	u.setInt("bvcb", 76)
